add_namespace = csa

### Constitution Events ###

###Social Patriots
country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Property Debate
	id = csa.1000
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1000"}
	title = csa.1000.t
	desc = csa.1000.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborists win out
		name = csa.1000.a	
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1001
			days = 7
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_afl
			value = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_browder
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # The Nationalists win out
		name = csa.1000.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1001
			days = 7
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_nationalists
			value = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_burnham
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Social Radicalism
	id = csa.1001
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1001"}
	title = csa.1001.t
	desc = csa.1001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborists win out
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1001.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.03
		}	
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1002
			days = 7
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_afl
			value = 1
				}
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_burnham
			value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	option = { # The Nationalists win out
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1001.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1002
			days = 7
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_nationalists
			value = 1
			}
			modify_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_browder
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - Voting Rights
	id = csa.1002
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1002"}
	title = csa.1002.t
	desc = csa.1002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Laborite Plan
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war

					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1002.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.08
		}
		country_event = {
			id = csa.1003
			days = 6
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
		}
		hidden_effect = {

			flag = CSA_afl
			value = 1
			}
		}
	}

				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {

country_event = { # Socialist Election Arrives
	id = csa.1003
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1003"}
	title = csa.1003.t
	desc = csa.1003.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #The Independence League
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.a
		trigger = {
		OR = {
		NOT = {
		has_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
		}
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_nationalists
			value > 2
			}
		}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
		id = csa.901
		days = 6
		}
		country_event = {
		id = csa.330
		days = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Victory
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # The AFL
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.b
		trigger = {
		OR = {
		has_country_flag = CSA_Laborite_Plan
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_afl
			value > 2
			}
		}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
		id = csa.901
		days = 6
		}
		country_event = {
		id = csa.325
		days = 5
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_AFL_In_Power
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Browder's SPA Centralist Ticket
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BURNHAM
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_LOVESTONE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.c
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_browder
			value > 2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
			id = csa.901
			days = 6
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BBR = {
						has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
					}
				}
				BBR = {
					country_event = {
						id = bbr.28
						days = 35
					}
				}
			}
			add_ideas = CSA_Ernest_Hemingway_for_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Gus_Hall_eco_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Steve_Nelson_sec_tot
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Earl Browder"
				desc = "POLITICS_EARL_BROWDER_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Earl_Bowder.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = popcom_subtype
				traits = { CSA_new_founding_father }
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.71
				days = 365
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.72
				days = 380
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.74
				days = 430
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party_long
			name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalists_in_power
		}
	}
	option = { # The American Worker's Party
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BROWDER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_NATIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FEDERALIST
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.1003.e
		trigger = {
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = CSA_burnham
			value > 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		country_event = {
		id = csa.901
		days = 6
		}
		set_country_flag = CSA_burnham_is_leader
		set_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
			add_ideas = CSA_Joseph_Zack_Kornfeder_for_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Frederick_L_Ackerman_eco_tot
			add_ideas = CSA_Lawrence_Dennis_sec_tot 
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "James Burnham"
				desc = "POLITICS_JAMES_BURNHAM_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_burnham.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = technocratic_socialism_subtype
				traits = { managerialist }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = csa.165 days = 8 }
				country_event = { id = csa.273 months = 2 }
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = totalist
			long_name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party_long
			name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BBR = {
					has_country_leader = { ruling_only = yes name = "Harry Haywood"}
				}
			}
			BBR = {
				country_event = {
					id = bbr.28
					days = 35
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Constitutional Convention begins
	id = csa.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.1"}
	title = csa.1.t
	desc = csa.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

    fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = bellamyism_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = syndicalist_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "CSA Central Committee"
				desc = "POLITICS_CSA_CENTRAL_COMITTEE_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_committee.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authcom_subtype
				traits = {
					our_right_to_survive
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_centralists
				value = 0
			}
			set_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_radicals
				value = 0
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Socialist Constitution - System of Government
	id = csa.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.2"}
	title = csa.2.t
	desc = csa.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		name = csa.2.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CSA_radicals_gain_power
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = totalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = CSA_radicals
				value = 1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.3
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_FOSTER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war
						option = CSA_POST_CIVIL_WAR_BUTLER
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CSA_post_civil_war

					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = csa.2.b

		}

			}

			}
		}
	}
}

	id = csa.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.3"}

	desc = { # Socialist
		text = csa.3.d.syndicalist
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
		}
	}
	desc = { # Syndicalism
		text = csa.3.d.socialist
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_party
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.3.a
		add_political_power = 20
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.5
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Constitutional Convention over
	id = csa.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.10"}

	desc = csa.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	option = {
		name = csa.10.a
		country_event = {
			id = csa.11
			days = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_syndicalism
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = totalist

					name = CSA_totalist_syndicalism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					long_name = CSA_syndicalist_party_syndicalism_long
					name = CSA_syndicalist_syndicalism_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party_long
					name = CSA_radical_socialist_syndicalism_party
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_socialist
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = totalist
					long_name = CSA_totalist_federalist_party_long
					name = CSA_totalist_federalist_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = syndicalist
					long_name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party_long
					name = CSA_syndicalist_federalist_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = radical_socialist
					long_name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party_long
					name = CSA_radical_socialist_federalist_party
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_chicago
			}
			set_capital = { state = 395 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_washington
			}
			set_capital = { state = 361 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_philly
			}
			set_capital = { state = 360 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_capital_nyc
			}
			set_capital = { state = 358 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1940 Election
	id = csa.29
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.29 FROM = [From.GetName]" }
	title = csa.29.t
	desc = csa.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		}
		date > 1940.1.1
		date < 1944.1.1
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.29.a
		increase_ruling_party_popularity_by_3 = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.28
				days = 1230
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.2905
				days = 1237
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.290
				days = 1242
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
	}
	desc = { # IWW does not have the Presidency
		text = csa.28.d.not_president

		}
	}

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist

		}
		NOT = {

			NOT = { has_government = syndicalist }

### 1948 Elections ###

country_event = { # 1948 IWW/SLP Primary
	id = csa.31
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.31"}
	title = csa.31.t
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	desc = { # IWW won the presidency just last time
		text = csa.31.d.president
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { # IWW won also in 1940
		text = csa.31.d.president_steps_down
		trigger = {
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
		}
	}
	desc = { # IWW does not have the Presidency
		text = csa.31.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = syndicalist
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Eric Hass
		name = csa.31.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = syndicalist
				}
				has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_ansynd
					has_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_ansynd
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_hass
			set_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
				}
				clr_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Elizabeth Nord
		name = csa.31.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = syndicalist
				}
				has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {

					has_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_ansynd

		hidden_effect = {

				}

			}
		}
	}

				}
				has_country_flag = csa_1944_election_syndie

			NOT = {

country_event = { # 1948 Election
	id = csa.33
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.33"}
	title = csa.33.t
	desc = csa.33.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			if = { # Eric Hass
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_hass }
				
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Eric Hass"
					desc = "POLITICS_ERIC_HASS_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Eric_Hass.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = de_leonism_subtype
					traits = {
						CSA_de_leonist
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Elizabeth Nord
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_nord }
				
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Elizabeth Nord"
					desc = "POLITICS_ELIZABETH_NORD_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Elizabeth_Nord.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
					female = yes
					traits = {
						indecisive
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Sam Dolgoff
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_iww_primary_dolgoff }
				
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Sam Dolgoff"
					desc = "POLITICS_DOLGOFF_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Sam_Dolgoff.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = anarcho_syndicalist_subtype
					female = yes
					traits = {
						anarchist_zeal
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Bayard Rustin
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_cio_primary_rustin }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Bayard Rustin"
					desc = "POLITICS_BAYARD_RUSTIN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Bayard_Rustin.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = bellamyism_subtype
					traits = {
						great_survivor
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Darlington Hoopes
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_cio_primary_hoopes }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Darlington Hoopes"
					desc = "POLITICS_DARLINGTON_HOOPES_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Darlington_Hoopes.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = bellamyism_subtype
					traits = {
						captain_of_industry
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Frank Zeidler
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_afl_primary_zeidler }

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Frank Zeidler"
					desc = "POLITICS_ZEIDLER_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Frank_Zeidler.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						CSA_the_american_haussmann
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Hugh Mulzac
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1948_afl_primary_mulzac }

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Hugh Mulzac"
					desc = "POLITICS_MULZAC_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_hugh_mulzac.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						hog_old_admiral
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # SocDem
		name = csa.33.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1948_election_socdem
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Thomas_Kennedy_for_sde
			CSA_Reuben_Soderstrom_eco_sde
			CSA_Frank_J_Hayes_sec_sde
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.3703
				days = 5
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.34
				days = 1230
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.35
				days = 1237
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.355
				days = 1242
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # RadSoc
		name = csa.33.b
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1948_election_radsoc
			set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Victory
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Asa_P_Randolph_for_rso
			CSA_John_L_Lewis_eco_rso
			CSA_Charles_Chaplin_sec_rso
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.39
				days = 5
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.34
				days = 1230
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.35
				days = 1237
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.355
				days = 1242
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Syndie
		name = csa.33.c
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1948_election_syndie
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_ansynd
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_election_ansynd
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_de_leonist
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_election_de_leonist
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = CSA_1944_election_orthodox
			}
			set_country_flag = CSA_1948_election_orthodox
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Ralph_Chaplin_for_syn
					CSA_Frank_Little_eco_syn
					CSA_Eugene_Dennis_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Carlo_Tresca_for_syn
					CSA_Wyndham_Mortimer_eco_syn
					CSA_Salaria_Kea_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Max_Shachtman_for_syn
					CSA_Harry_Bridges_eco_syn
					CSA_Lee_Pressman_sec_syn
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.39
				days = 5
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.34
				days = 1230
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.35
				days = 1237
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.355
				days = 1242
			}
		}
	}
}

			has_government = social_democrat
			has_country_flag = csa_1948_election_socdem
		}
	}
	desc = { # CIO does not have the Presidency
		text = csa.355.d.not_president
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
		}
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Daniel Hoan
		name = csa.355.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				has_country_flag = csa_1948_election_socdem
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_1952_afl_primary_hoan
		}
	}
	option = { # George Meany
		name = csa.355.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
				has_country_flag = csa_1948_election_socdem
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CSA_1952_afl_primary_meany
		}
	}
	option = { # Nominate the President
		name = csa.355.e
		trigger = {
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # 1952 Election
	id = csa.36
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.36"}
	title = csa.36.t
	desc = csa.36.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_election_vote

	trigger = {
		tag = CSA
		has_country_flag = CSA_constitutional_convention_done
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1940_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1944_election
		has_country_flag = CSA_had_1948_election
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = radical_socialist
			has_government = syndicalist
			has_government = social_democrat
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { # Eugene Dennis
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_dennis }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Eugene Dennis"
					desc = "POLITICS_EUGENE_DENNIS_DESC"

						indecisive
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Henning A. Blomen
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_blomen }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Henning A. Blomen"
					desc = "POLITICS_HENNING_BLOMEN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Henning_A_Blomen.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = anarcho_syndicalist_subtype
					traits = {
						CSA_bloodless_revolutionary
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # John Bernard
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_iww_primary_bernard }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "John Bernard"
					desc = "POLITICS_JOHN_BERNARD_DESC"

					expire = "1965.1.1"

					traits = {
						warmonger
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Oakley C. Johnson
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_cio_primary_johnson }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Oakley C. Johnson"
					desc = "POLITICS_OAKLEY_JOHNSON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Oakley_C_Johnson.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = bellamyism_subtype
					traits = {
						editor
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Noam Chomsky
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_cio_primary_chomsky }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Noam Chomsky"
					desc = "POLITICS_NOAM_CHOMSKY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Noam_Chomsky.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = radsoc_anarcho_syndicalist_subtype
					traits = {
						anarchist_zeal
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # Daniel Hoan
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_afl_primary_hoan }

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Daniel Hoan"
					desc = "POLITICS_HOAN_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Daniel_Hoan.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						CSA_sewer_socialism
					}
				}
			}
			if = { # George Meany
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_1952_afl_primary_meany }

				create_country_leader = {
					name = "George Meany"
					desc = "POLITICS_MEANY_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_George_Meany.png"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = syndie_social_democrat_subtype
					traits = {
						trade_union_boss
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # SocDem
		name = csa.33.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_socdem
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Thomas_Kennedy_for_sde
			CSA_Reuben_Soderstrom_eco_sde
			CSA_Frank_J_Hayes_sec_sde
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.3703
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # IWW
		name = csa.36.a
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_iww
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = syndicalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_orthodx_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Ralph_Chaplin_for_syn
					CSA_Frank_Little_eco_syn
					CSA_Eugene_Dennis_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_ansynd_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Carlo_Tresca_for_syn
					CSA_Wyndham_Mortimer_eco_syn
					CSA_Salaria_Kea_sec_syn
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CSA_de_leonist_leadership }
				remove_all_ministers_but_hog = yes
				add_ideas = {
					CSA_Max_Shachtman_for_syn
					CSA_Harry_Bridges_eco_syn
					CSA_Lee_Pressman_sec_syn
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.40
				days = 1
			}
			#no more primaries
		}
	}
	option = { # CIO
		name = csa.36.c
		set_country_flag = CSA_had_1952_election
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = csa_1952_election_cio
			set_country_flag = CSA_Nationalist_Victory
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			election_frequency = 48
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		add_ideas = {
			CSA_Asa_P_Randolph_for_rso
			CSA_John_L_Lewis_eco_rso
			CSA_Charles_Chaplin_sec_rso
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.40
				days = 1
			}
			#no more primaries
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Appointing a Second in Command
	id = csa.50
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.50"}
	title = { # Browder's Second in Command
		text = csa.50.t.browder
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Earl Browder"
			}
		}
	}
	title = { # Foster's Second in Command
		text = csa.50.t.foster
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "William Z. Foster"
			}
		}
	}
	title = { # Burnham's Second in Command
		text = csa.50.t.burnham
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes

			}
		}

		tag = CSA
		has_government = totalist

			has_country_leader = {

			}

				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Earl Browder"
			}
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "James Burnham"
			}
		}
	}

		add_ideas = CSA_John_J_Ballam_hog_tot

			}
		}

			}
		}
		add_ideas = CSA_Jay_Fox_hog_tot
	}
	option = { # William Weinstone
		name = csa.50.e

			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "William Z. Foster"
			}
		}
		add_ideas = CSA_William_Weinstone_hog_tot
	}
	### Browder's Men ###
	option = { # Max Bedacht
		name = csa.50.f

country_event = { # Overtures to Mexico
	id = csa.130
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.130"}
	title = csa.130.t
	desc = csa.130.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = csa.130.a #Agree
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_opinion = {
					target = FROM
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = USA_american_trade
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_likes_govt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					is_guaranteed_by = FROM
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				give_guarantee = MEX
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					gives_military_access_to = FROM
				}
			}
			give_military_access = FROM
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_mainland_america = yes
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = MEX
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_claimed_by = MEX
				}
				remove_claim_by = MEX
			}
			CSA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = FROM
						is_claimed_by = FROM
					}
					is_mainland_america = no
					is_core_of = MEX
				}
				MEX = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = csa.131
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = csa.130.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_subject_of = FROM
					is_in_faction_with = FROM
					has_opinion = {
						target = FROM
						value > 50
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = ITA_dislikes_govt
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = csa.132
				hours = 8
			}
		}
	}
}

				hidden_effect = {

				days = 50
						}
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1 }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_1
					add_idea = CSA_iron_brigades_idea_reinforced
				}
				hidden_effect = {
				CSA = {

country_event = { # La Internationale
	id = csa.500
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa.500"}
	title = csa.500.t
	desc = csa.500.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Send Funds
	name = csa.500.a
	add_political_power = -40
	FRA = {
	add_political_power = 40
	add_opinion_modifier = { target = CSA modifier = small_increase }
		}
	}
	option = { # Send Military Aid
	name = csa.500.b
	add_political_power = -40
	add_manpower = -15000
	add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
		type = infantry_equipment
		amount = -5000
		producer = CSA
	}
	add_opinion_modifier = { target = CSA modifier = medium_increase }
	FRA = {
	add_political_power = 40
	add_manpower = 15000
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 5000
			producer = CSA
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Disavow them
	name = csa.500.c
	add_political_power = 30
	decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_5 = yes
	add_opinion_modifier = { target = CSA modifier = medium_decrease }
	}
	option = { # Non-Aggression
	name = csa.500.e
	diplomatic_relation = {
    country = FRA
    relation = non_aggression_pact
    active = yes
		}
	}
}

		add_political_power = 20

	}
}

country_event = { # Take a Vacation?
	id = csa_sucsessor.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa_sucsessor.1"}
	title = csa_sucsessor.1.t
	desc = csa_sucsessor.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_USA_congress

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = { #yes
		name = csa_sucsessor.1.a	
		
	}

	option = { #no
		name = csa_sucsessor.1.b	
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Earl Browder"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = csa_sucsessor.3
					days = 33
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "William Z. Foster"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = csa_sucsessor.4
					days = 33
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "James Burnham"
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = csa_sucsessor.2
					days = 33
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Death of Burnham
	id = csa_sucsessor.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event csa_sucsessor.2"}
	title = csa_sucsessor.2.t
	desc = csa_sucsessor.2.d
	picture = GFX_event_CSA_burnham
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = CSA_James_Burnham_hog_tot }
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = CSA_James_Burnham_hog_tot
					add_idea = CSA_Howard_Scott_hog_tot
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { #Lovestone 
		name = csa_sucsessor.2.a	
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Jay Lovestone"
			desc = "POLITICS_JAY_LOVESTONE_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Jay_Lovestone.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = lovestoneism_subtype
			traits = { trade_union_boss }
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = CSA_lovestone_1
	}
	
	option = { #Cannon
		name = csa_sucsessor.2.b	
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "James P. Cannon"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_James_P_Cannon.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = technocratic_socialism_subtype
			traits = { }
		}
	}

	option = { #Reagan
		name = csa_sucsessor.2.c
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Lyndon LaRouche"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/CSA/Portrait_CSA_Lyndon_LaRouche.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = technocratic_socialism_subtype
			traits = { hog_militant_reactionary }
		}
	}

	option = { #LaRouche
		name = csa_sucsessor.2.e	
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Ronald Reagan"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/USA/Portrait_USA_Ronald_Reagan.png"
			expire = "1965.1.1"
			ideology = technocratic_socialism_subtype
			traits = { eco_patriotic_socialist }
		}
	}
}
